{: .only-website }
  *This is a work in progress jointly with Marc Bezem.*

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: .equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

Using the flattening lemma we can prove this equivalence:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1013" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1017" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="1025" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="1037" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="1042" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="1047" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="1054" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>
<a id="1075" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="1082" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">_</a> <a id="1084" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point and one no trivial path
called *path* as we can see in the following picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png){: width="%30" }
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

Induction principle on paths:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2543" class="Comment">-- Postulate.</a>

## `pS` type

The `pS` type as the figure below shows, it is a circle with two edges
in opposite direction between two points. Notice this HIT is just different
form the suspension of booleans (Σ 2) by reversing one arrow.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/tour-type.png){: width="%40" }
*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

## S¹ ≃ pS

**Lemma 1** . $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

####  f ∘ g ~ id

To prove the homotopy $$ f ∘ g \sim \mathsf{id}$$,
we prove for the pS₁ case and the case for paths.

- Case on pS₁:

{: .foldable until="2" }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5852" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>

    <a id="9067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#8384" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Finally, by path induction on `pS` type, we got the homotopy.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9159" class="Comment">-- Homotopy.</a>
  <a id="Lemma₁.H₁"></a><a id="9174" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#9174" class="Function">H₁</a> <a id="9177" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9179" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5526" class="Function">f</a> <a id="9181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4146" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="9183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5605" class="Function">g</a> <a id="9185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#26688" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="9187" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3616" class="Function">id</a>
  <a id="9192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#9174" class="Function">H₁</a> <a id="9195" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9197" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#4340" class="Function">pS-ind</a> <a id="9204" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="9206" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9207" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5693" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="9212" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3315" class="Function">pS₀</a><a id="9215" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9217" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5862" class="Function">q₁</a> <a id="9220" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5989" class="Function">dpath₀</a> <a id="9227" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#7455" class="Function">dpath₁</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

####  g ∘ f ~ id

To prove this homotopy $$g ∘ f \sim \mathsf{id}$$, we proceed by induction on
the circle. For the `base` case, `refl base` works since `g (f base)` is
definitionally equal to `base`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9463" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
  <a id="Lemma₁.H₂-base"></a><a id="9473" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#9473" class="Function">H₂-base</a> <a id="9481" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1517" class="Function">base</a> <a id="9488" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5527" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="9491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1517" class="Function">base</a>
  <a id="9498" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#9473" class="Function">H₂-base</a> <a id="9506" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9508" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#5693" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="9513" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1517" class="Function">base</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The rest is how we prove the case for action on `loop`.

We will need the term `aux-path` which is:

{: .foldable until="2"}

{: .foldable until="2" }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9998" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>

## Action on paths of pairs

Action on paths of pairs appears as Lemma 6.12.7 in {% cite hottbook %}.

Let's define out context for this lemma:

And this lemma says:

##  Σ S¹ P ≃ pS

**Lemma 3.** $$ \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS $$ where
$$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13250" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Lemma₃"></a><a id="13257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13257" class="Module">Lemma₃</a> <a id="13264" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="13271" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>

Now, using the negation function as an equivalence, we define the family of types `P`
over the circle S¹.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="P"></a><a id="13587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13587" class="Function">P</a> <a id="13589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1492" class="Function">S¹</a> <a id="13594" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13596" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1025" class="Function">Type₀</a>
<a id="13602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13587" class="Function">P</a> <a id="13604" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1868" class="Function">S¹-rec</a> <a id="13613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1025" class="Function">Type₀</a> <a id="13619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3088" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="13624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#50944" class="Function">ua</a> <a id="13628" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13333" class="Function">neg-eq</a><a id="13634" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Two auxiliar lemmas for the latter:

### g ∘ f ∼ id

Taking inspiration from Flattening lemma's proof in Section 6
in {% cite hottbook %}, we got the following proof.

Finally, the equivalence:
